Codex-ManagersOffice\AGENTS.md:1:# Repository Guidelines
Codex-ManagersOffice\AGENTS.md:2:
Codex-ManagersOffice\AGENTS.md:3:## Project Structure & Module Organization
Codex-ManagersOffice\AGENTS.md:4:- Frontend lives in `src`; React entry is `src/main.jsx` and `src/App.jsx`, with UI
split into `src/components/AFE`, `src/components/Scheduler`, `src/components/Scouting`, and `src/components/Terminal`.
Codex-ManagersOffice\AGENTS.md:5:- State is kept in `src/state` via small Zustand stores; extend these rather than
adding ad-hoc globals.
Codex-ManagersOffice\AGENTS.md:6:- Shared styling starts at `src/styles/global.css`; add component-scoped styles
nearby when needed.
Codex-ManagersOffice\AGENTS.md:7:- Backend sits in `backend`; `backend/server.js` is the Express entry, with domain
helpers in `backend/core`, HTTP handlers in `backend/routes`, and service clients in `backend/services`.
Codex-ManagersOffice\AGENTS.md:8:- `codex-builder.cjs` seeds or expands the scaffold (see commands) when you need to
regenerate baseline files.
Codex-ManagersOffice\AGENTS.md:9:
Codex-ManagersOffice\AGENTS.md:10:## Build, Test, and Development Commands
Codex-ManagersOffice\AGENTS.md:11:- `node codex-builder.cjs --mission=FULL_STACK_SCAFFOLD_V2` regenerates the minimal
full-stack scaffold.
Codex-ManagersOffice\AGENTS.md:12:- `node codex-builder.cjs --mission=FULL_STACK_COMPONENT_EXPANSION_V3` writes the
expanded component/agent set.
Codex-ManagersOffice\AGENTS.md:13:- `npm install` (root) installs frontend/backend deps once `package.json` is
present; use Node 18+.
Codex-ManagersOffice\AGENTS.md:14:- `npm run dev` to serve the React frontend (Vite-style setup) and `node
backend/server.js` to run the API on 5001.
Codex-ManagersOffice\AGENTS.md:15:- `npm test` for the test suite once added (see Testing Guidelines).
Codex-ManagersOffice\AGENTS.md:16:
Codex-ManagersOffice\AGENTS.md:17:## Coding Style & Naming Conventions
Codex-ManagersOffice\AGENTS.md:18:- Use ES modules on the frontend and keep functions as small, pure React components;
backend currently uses CommonJS.
Codex-ManagersOffice\AGENTS.md:19:- Prefer 2-space indentation, single quotes in JS/JSX, and camelCase for
variables/functions; PascalCase for components.
Codex-ManagersOffice\AGENTS.md:20:- Keep filenames descriptive by feature (e.g., `SchedulerPanel.jsx`,
`useScheduleStore.js`).
Codex-ManagersOffice\AGENTS.md:21:- Type hints are absent; document expectations with JSDoc-style comments when
behavior is non-obvious.
Codex-ManagersOffice\AGENTS.md:22:
Codex-ManagersOffice\AGENTS.md:23:## Testing Guidelines
Codex-ManagersOffice\AGENTS.md:24:- Add React component tests with Vitest + Testing Library (`*.test.jsx` near
components) and backend route tests with supertest (`backend/**/*.test.js`).
Codex-ManagersOffice\AGENTS.md:25:- Aim for coverage on new logic branches (stores, services, route handlers); stub
external calls in `backend/services`.
Codex-ManagersOffice\AGENTS.md:26:- Run `npm test` locally before opening a PR; include expected outputs or fixtures.
Codex-ManagersOffice\AGENTS.md:27:
Codex-ManagersOffice\AGENTS.md:28:## Commit & Pull Request Guidelines
Codex-ManagersOffice\AGENTS.md:29:- Write imperative, scoped commits; Conventional Commit style is preferred (e.g.,
`feat: add terminal input bar`).
Codex-ManagersOffice\AGENTS.md:30:- PRs should describe motivation, key changes, and manual test notes; attach
screenshots/GIFs for UI work and list affected routes for backend changes.
Codex-ManagersOffice\AGENTS.md:31:- Link issues/task IDs when available and keep PRs focused on a single concern.
Codex-ManagersOffice\AGENTS.md:32:
Codex-ManagersOffice\AGENTS.md:33:## Security & Configuration Tips
Codex-ManagersOffice\AGENTS.md:34:- Do not commit secrets; use environment variables and a local `.env` (keep it
untracked).
Codex-ManagersOffice\AGENTS.md:35:- CORS is enabled in `backend/server.js`; tighten origins when deploying beyond
local.
Codex-ManagersOffice\AGENTS.md:36:- Network ports: frontend defaults to 5173 (if Vite) and backend to 5001; document
if you change them.
Codex-ManagersOffice\ARCHITECTURE.md:1:# Project Codex  Manager-First Architecture (Canonical)
Codex-ManagersOffice\ARCHITECTURE.md:2:
Codex-ManagersOffice\ARCHITECTURE.md:3:## Status
Codex-ManagersOffice\ARCHITECTURE.md:4:- Date: 2025-12-13

Codex-ManagersOffice\ARCHITECTURE.md:7:
Codex-ManagersOffice\ARCHITECTURE.md:8:## Core
Codex-ManagersOffice\ARCHITECTURE.md:9:- Single authoritative engine (bootstrap + autopilot + heartbeat)
Codex-ManagersOffice\ARCHITECTURE.md:10:- Heartbeat verified live
Codex-ManagersOffice\ARCHITECTURE.md:11:- Autopilot guarded by lock
Codex-ManagersOffice\ARCHITECTURE.md:12:
Codex-ManagersOffice\ARCHITECTURE.md:13:## Interface
Codex-ManagersOffice\ARCHITECTURE.md:14:- Canonical Manager UI:
Codex-ManagersOffice\ARCHITECTURE.md:15:  C:\Users\Asus\Documents\Codex-ManagersOffice\frontend\frontend
Codex-ManagersOffice\ARCHITECTURE.md:16:- Purpose: Observe, decide, step back
Codex-ManagersOffice\ARCHITECTURE.md:17:- No execution authority in UI
Codex-ManagersOffice\ARCHITECTURE.md:18:
Codex-ManagersOffice\ARCHITECTURE.md:19:## Layers
Codex-ManagersOffice\ARCHITECTURE.md:20:1. Codex Core (authoritative, headless)
Codex-ManagersOffice\ARCHITECTURE.md:21:2. Manager / Monitor UI (AFE, AgentChip, Terminal, Scheduler)
Codex-ManagersOffice\ARCHITECTURE.md:22:3. Game / Simulation UI (sandboxed, non-authoritative)
Codex-ManagersOffice\ARCHITECTURE.md:23:
Codex-ManagersOffice\ARCHITECTURE.md:24:## Design Philosophy
Codex-ManagersOffice\ARCHITECTURE.md:25:Inspired by Football Manager:
Codex-ManagersOffice\ARCHITECTURE.md:26:- Indirect control
Codex-ManagersOffice\ARCHITECTURE.md:27:- Agent trust
Codex-ManagersOffice\ARCHITECTURE.md:28:- Reports over micromanagement
Codex-ManagersOffice\ARCHITECTURE.md:29:- One engine, many views
Codex-ManagersOffice\ARCHITECTURE.md:30:
Codex-ManagersOffice\ARCHITECTURE.md:31:## Declaration
Codex-ManagersOffice\ARCHITECTURE.md:32:This document freezes the first stable Codex Manager runtime.
